repeatedly, because of the uppercase of `UTF8` :\r\n\r\n```\r\nTerraform will perform the following actions:\r\n\r\n  # alicloud_db_database.example must be replaced\r\n-/+ resource repeatedly, because of the uppercase of `UTF8` :\r\n\r\n```\r\nTerraform will perform the following actions:\r\n\r\n  # alicloud_db_database.example must be replaced\r\n-/+ resource  instance_id   = \"pgm-abcdefghijklmnop\"\r\n        name          = \"example\"\r\n    }\r\n```\r\n\r\nThe `db_instance` is using:\r\n\r\n```\r\n  engine           = \"PostgreSQL\"\r\n
